[30;1m4 | [0m[35m    Adds a basic http auth middleware as an alternative to noauth in[0m
[30;1m5 | [0m[35m    standalone environments. This middleware uses a password file which[0m
[30;1m6 | [0m[35m    supports the Apache `htpasswd`_ syntax. This file is read for every[0m
[30;1m7 | [0m[35m    request, so no service restart is required when changes are made.[0m
[30;1m8 | [0m[35m    The only password digest supported is bcrypt, and the ``bcrypt``[0m
[30;1m9 | [0m[35m    python library is used for password checks since it supports ``$2y$``[0m
[30;1m10 | [0m[35m    prefixed bcrypt passwords as generated by the Apache htpasswd utility.[0m
